              A MIGRANT at the southern border warned that the current surge in asylum seekers is 'never going to stop' as the White House blames Donald Trump for the growing crisis.

            <a class="text-anchor-wrap" href="https://www.the-sun.com/uncategorized/2556084/modeller-golf-ball-images-e-t-donald-trump-yoda/">
             <h2 class="teaser__headline t-p-color">
              IT’S E.T. TO A TEE
             </h2>
             <p class="teaser__subdeck">
              Modeller makes golf-ball images of E.T, Donald Trump and Yoda
             </p>
             <h2 class="teaser__lead">
              MODELLER Tony Amatruda, 82, of Basingstoke, Hants, moulds clay on to old balls to ­create characters. He said: 'My skills as a prosthetic technician come in handy.'
             </h2>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="article-data teaser__social">
            <div class="article-data__item article-data__share" data-url="https://www.the-sun.com/uncategorized/2556084/modeller-golf-ball-images-e-t-donald-trump-yoda/">
             <a href="https://www.the-sun.com/uncategorized/2556084/modeller-golf-ball-images-e-t-donald-trump-yoda/">
              <svg height="15" width="16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

             <h2 class="teaser__headline t-p-color">
              'WILLY' TOY
             </h2>
             <p class="teaser__subdeck">
              Mom stunned to find toy bought for daughter, 10, shaped like a penis
             </p>
             <h2 class="teaser__lead">
              A MOM was left stunned after finding out the stress-busting fidget toy she had bought for her daughter looked like a penis. Leanne Dransfield, 30, paid for a mixed pack of the toys for Maisie, ten. Leanne says 'I had no idea what was in her pack until we sat down.'

            <a class="text-anchor-wrap" href="https://www.the-sun.com/news/2555745/ruby-blackburn-woolkies-terrier-nel-pet-lamb-brian/">
             <h2 class="teaser__headline t-p-color">
              BAAA-KING MAD
             </h2>
             <p class="teaser__subdeck">
              Adorable girl, 4, goes walkies with terrier Nel and her pet lamb Brian
             </p>
             <h2 class="teaser__lead">
              AN ORPHANED lamb has a spring back in his step after being adopted by a four-year-old girl who takes him for walks with her border terrier Nel and bulldog Brooke. Brian the lamb was taken in after his mum and sister died at the start of the month. He now loves nothing more than walkies with his two new furry pals.
             </h2>
            </a>
           </div>
